## Dataflow & Wiring

- Entry points: `market_monitor.cli` (CLI), PowerShell scripts (`run.ps1`, `run_all.ps1`).
- Config loading: `market_monitor.config_schema` reads YAML/TOML/JSON and env overrides.
- Providers: offline NASDAQ daily provider (`market_monitor.providers.nasdaq_daily`) or online providers.
- Pipeline: `market_monitor.cli.run_pipeline` -> `stage_pipeline` (staging, gates, features, themes, risk).
- Features: `market_monitor.features.compute_features` produces trend/regime/tail/attention/data-quality fields.
- Scoring: `market_monitor.scoring.score_frame` outputs monitor score and components.
- Outputs: CSVs + `run_report.md` + optional predictions + model card.

## Schema Contracts

- Canonical OHLCV columns: `Date`, `Open`, `High`, `Low`, `Close`, `Volume` (Volume may be NA).
- Feature outputs defined in `market_monitor.io.FEATURE_COLUMNS`.
- Scored outputs defined in `market_monitor.io.SCORED_COLUMNS`.
- External data env vars: `MARKET_APP_DATA_ROOT`, `MARKET_APP_NASDAQ_DAILY_DIR`, `MARKET_APP_SILVER_PRICES_DIR`, `OFFLINE_MODE`.

## Tests & Coverage

- Pytest suite in `tests/` covering gates, features, scoring, and smoke pipeline.
- Coverage not currently enforced; no coverage report configured.
